                        <span style="padding-left: 5px;">
                            <strong style="font-size:15pt;">Michael Blazek</strong></span>
                        <div class="spacer_10"></div>
                        <div style="font-size: 10pt; padding-left: 5px;">

                        </div>
                    </td>
                    
                    <tr style="background-color: #FFF;"><td style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; font-size:10pt;"><div style="padding-top:5px; padding-bottom:5px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px;"><b><a href="http://www.rotowire.com/users/ad_jump.asp?id=688&playerid=12637" style="text-decoration:none;">RotoWire News</a>:</b> Blazek will start Milwaukee's game against the Nationals on Thursday.                 <tr id="so1" style="background-color: #FFF;"><td colspan="5" style="border-top:2px solid #D3D3D3; padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="width:100%; font-size:10pt"><center>Profiles:&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa6" href="javascript:showMoreSO2014();">2014</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa8" href="javascript:showMoreSO2016();">2016</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a id="soa9"  href="javascript:showMoreSO2017();">2017</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;(Click Year to Expand / <a href="javascript:hideSO('so1');">Close</a>)</center></div></td></tr>
                
                
                
                
                <tr id="so6" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Blazek possesses big velocity, as well as big command issues. His walk rate historically has been lofty in the minors, and in 17.1 innings with the Brewers, the right-hander posted 6.75 walks per nine. Sprinkle in a few home runs and an unsightly 5.71 ERA, and it clearly wasn't a successful major-league debut. As such, Blazek isn't guaranteed to break camp with the Brewers and shouldn't come anywhere near your fantasy roster. (JP Breen)</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                
                <tr id="so8" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>Blazek's 2015 came to an early end due to a hand fracture, but it isn't expected to affect him going into this season. The 26-year old had a strong rookie season last year, and will likely be an important piece of the Brewers bullpen in 2016. Blazek isn't exactly a flamethrower, with a fastball sitting in the lower 90s. He doesn't pile up the strikeouts, and there's always the danger that the control problems he displayed in the minors (3.78 walks per nine in 629 innings pitched) flare up in the majors. (Scott Strandberg)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>He'll get some holds, but there's far better options out there.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
                <tr id="so9" style="background-color: #FFF; display:none;"><td colspan="5" padding:3px; text-align:justify;"><div class="m_stories" style="font-size:10pt"><center><table><tr><td style="width:615px; padding-right:7px; text-align:justify;" valign="top"><b>Profile: </b>What happens when you walk too many guys with a fly ball rate approaching 40%? See Blazek's 2016. After a productive though unremarkable 2015, Blazek struggled with command and the long ball in 2016. A .349 batting average on balls in play may have exacerbated some of his problems, but even if we regress it to league average, there are still too many baserunners and fly balls here, and that's manifested in his FIP, xFIP, and DRA. Blazek doesn't strike out enough batters to be worthy as a middle reliever, and he's too buried on the Milwaukee depth chart to reasonably expect any saves. (Rylan Edwards)<br /><br /><b>The Quick Opinion: </b>Even with a nice pitch mix for a reliever, there's no upside here. Blazek  needs to prove 2016's spike in walks was just aberrative and that the strong ground ball rates he exhibited in 2015 were for real. There's no reason he should occupy a spot on your roster while he attempts to do so.</td></tr></table></center></div></td></tr>
            </table>
